
Concepts predefined in the database
...................................

In our database design, the CONCEPT_DIMENSION plays a key role in defining the nature of observations derived from various sources such as LOINC or Snomed/CT. Each concept is identified by a unique CONCEPT_CD, which serves as a definitive code for the observed data. To further specify the type of data an observation contains, we introduce the VALTYPE_CD field.

The VALTYPE_CD field adopts several encoding types to capture a wide range of data, which are as follows

- N: Coded for numeric data.
- T: Coded for textual data.
- D: Encoded for date types and follows the YYYY-MM-DD format.
- R: Coded for raw data, to accommodate unprocessed or unformatted information directly from the data source. This type is used for variable images and other binary data.
- F: Coded for findings, indicating whether a particular clinical feature is present, with options such as 'yes', 'no' and 'unknown'.
- S: Coded for choices, often showing answers attached in the CONCEPT_PATH.
- A: Coded for answers to choices ('S'), often showing answers attached in the CONCEPT_PATH

If necessary, a unit is provided in the UNIT_CD field. A source system CUSTOM is also used to indicate that the concept has been added by us to capture additional information.

The CONCEPT_PATH enables the grouping of concepts into a hierarchical structure.

This table-driven approach allows for robust, efficient and flexible management of clinical observations while keeping the system intuitive to the end user.

.. NOTE::

    Each Concept of the VALTYPE_CD = 'S' has a predefined set of answers attached in the CONCEPT_PATH. For example, the concept "CONCEPT_CD": "SCTID: 263495000" (`Gender`) has the following answers:

    =====================================================   ==========================   =============
    Path                                                    Concept Code                 Concept Name
    =====================================================   ==========================   =============
    \\SNOMED-CT\\363787003\\278844005 \\263495000	        SCTID: 263495000	         Gender
    \\SNOMED-CT\\363787003\\278844005 \\263495000\\LA\\1	SCTID: 248152002	         Female
    \\SNOMED-CT\\363787003\\278844005 \\263495000\\LA\\2	SCTID: 248153007	         Male
    \\SNOMED-CT\\363787003\\278844005 \\263495000\\LA\\3    SCTID: 32570691000036108	 Intersex
    \\SNOMED-CT\\363787003\\278844005 \\263495000\\LA\\4	SCTID: 407374003	         Transsexual
    =====================================================   ==========================   =============
